# to FRANCE
# ENG, SPR/U35, CAN, AST, U02, SAF, BEL, HOL

event = { 
	id = 4000200
	random = no 
	persistent = yes
	tag = { ENG }

	trigger = {
		ai = yes
		atwar = yes
		alliance = { country = FRA }
		ai = FRA

		#We ceded control of our army
		NOT = { army = { size = 60 type = 1 which = 0 } }

		#FRA hasn't ceded control of its army
		army = { size = 50 type = 1 which = 0 country = FRA }
		
		region = { region = "France" country = FRA value = 30 }

		OR = {
			#At least 5 divisions sent
			AND = {
				NOT = { flag = exp_FRA_from_ENG_5 }
				ic = 10
				army = { size = 20 type = 1 which = 1 }
			}
			#At least 10 divisions sent
			AND = { 
				NOT = { flag = exp_FRA_from_ENG_10 }
				ic = 20
				army = { size = 40 type = 1 which = 1 }
			}
			AND = { 
				#At least 20 divisions sent
				NOT = { flag = exp_FRA_from_ENG_20 }
				ic = 40
				army = { size = 50 type = 1 which = 1 }
			}
			AND = { 
				#At least 40 divisions sent
				NOT = { flag = exp_FRA_from_ENG_40 }
				ic = 60
				army = { size = 70 type = 1 which = 1 }
			}
			AND = { 
				#At least 80 divisions sent
				NOT = { flag = exp_FRA_from_ENG_80 }
				ic = 100
				army = { size = 110 type = 1 which = 1 }
			}
			AND = { 
				#At least 160 divisions sent
				NOT = { flag = exp_FRA_from_ENG_160 }
				ic = 160
				army = { size = 190 type = 1 which = 1 }
			}
			AND = {
				#Not 5 divisions sent
				flag = exp_FRA_from_ENG_5
				NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 20 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 10 } }
			}
			AND = {
				#Not 10 divisions sent
				flag = exp_FRA_from_ENG_10
				NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 40 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 15 } }
			}
			AND = { 
				#Not 20 divisions sent
				flag = exp_FRA_from_ENG_20
				NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 50 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 30 } }
			}
			AND = { 
				#Not 40 divisions sent
				flag = exp_FRA_from_ENG_40
				NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 70 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 50 } }
			}

			}
		}
	}

	name = "Supplying our allies - adjustment"
 	desc = "Our allies need help supplying their army"
	style = 0 

	#DISABLED - WILL USE LEND LEASE
	#date = { day = 1 month = october year = 1913 }
	#offset = 5
	#deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

event = { 
	id = 4000700
	random = no 
	persistent = yes
	tag = { CHC }

	trigger = {
		ai = yes
		atwar = yes
		alliance = { country = CHI }
		ai = CHI

		#We ceded control of our army
		NOT = { army = { size = 50 type = 1 which = 0 } }
		
		OR = {
			#At least 5 divisions sent
			AND = {
				NOT = { flag = exp_CHI_from_CHC_5 }
				ic = 10
				army = { size = 40 type = 1 which = 1 }
			}
			#At least 10 divisions sent
			AND = { 
				NOT = { flag = exp_CHI_from_CHC_10 }
				ic = 20
				army = { size = 50 type = 1 which = 1 }
			}
			AND = { 
				#At least 20 divisions sent
				NOT = { flag = exp_CHI_from_CHC_20 }
				ic = 40
				army = { size = 70 type = 1 which = 1 }
			}
			AND = { 
				#At least 40 divisions sent
				NOT = { flag = exp_CHI_from_CHC_40 }
				ic = 60
				army = { size = 110 type = 1 which = 1 }
			}
			AND = { 
				#At least 80 divisions sent
				NOT = { flag = exp_CHI_from_CHC_80 }
				ic = 100
				army = { size = 190 type = 1 which = 1 }
			}
			AND = { 
				#At least 160 divisions sent
				NOT = { flag = exp_CHI_from_CHC_160 }
				ic = 160
				army = { size = 250 type = 1 which = 1 }
			}
			AND = {
				#Not 5 divisions sent
				flag = exp_CHI_from_CHC_5
				NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 40 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 10 } }
			}
			AND = {
				#Not 10 divisions sent
				flag = exp_CHI_from_CHC_10
				NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 50 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 15 } }
			}
			AND = { 
				#Not 20 divisions sent
				flag = exp_CHI_from_CHC_20
				NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 70 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 30 } }

	offset = 5
